 The monsoon rainfall so far has been 103 per cent of the normal
 yani saamaanya se zyada barish
 The best rains directly affect the crops of our country's farmers
 is baar acchhee barish kaa asar kharif fasalon kii buvaai par dikhaai de rahaa he
 Sowing area of kharif crops so far is about 58 as compared to last year
 27 lakh hectare zyada rahaa he
 Sowing area increased due to heavy rains According to the latest data of the Ministry of Agriculture, the total sowing area of kharif so far is 954

 baat ye he ki is saal dalhan ke buvaai rakabe main joardaar badhotaree dekhi gai he

 17 lakh hectare rahaa he

 The Government of India has made some changes in the pattern of JEE Mains Examination from the year 2017
 ejineering under graduate corcej main daakhile ke liye hone vaali sanyukt pravesh pariksha (jeii) main ranking nirdhaaran main 12veen kaksha ke ank nirdharak tatv nahin honge
 That is, from 2017, there will be no roll of numbers in JEE ranking in class 12th
 iske alaava jeii (advance) / jeii (main) ranking ke aadhaar par undergraduate ejineering corcej main admician dene vaale iaiti / enaiti / iiiti or anya kendriya vittiya sahaayta praapt takneekee sansthaanon ke liye qualifi karne ke liye bhi 12veen kaksha main kam se kam 75 fisadi marks hona anivaary he
 Or be in the top 20 percentile in the 12th grade examination conducted by the concerned board
 anusuchit jati, anusuchit janajati sanvarg ke liye yah yogyata 65 pratishat he
 The comments gauratlab he ki desh ke tamaam enaiti, iiiti, anya kendriya vittiya sahaayta praapt takneekee sansthaanon, is system main shaamil ho chuke rajyon ke sansthaanon or anya dheron sansthaanon main jeii (main) pariksha ke pradarshan ke aadhaar par ejineering undergraduate corcej main daakhila hota he
 On the basis of performance in JEE (main), there is an opportunity to take the JEE Advanced exam
 jeii advance pariksha ke jariye hi desh ke pratishthit santhaan iaiti ke ejineering corcej main daakhila liya ja saktaa he

 Describing casteism as a bitter reality of the country, Congress Vice President Rahul Gandhi today said that the dream of ending the casteism of the constitution maker Dr
 Bhimrao Ambedkar is still incomplete and some divisive ideologies are trying to strengthen the walls of casteism
 rahul ne ambedkar kii varsh 2016 main manaai jane vaali 125 veen jainti ke maddenjar congress ke varmbhar chalane vaale kaaryakramon kii yahaan aupchaarik shuruyaat kii
 He made his address on the occasion with the slogan 'jai Bhim' at the general meeting held at the Swarg Mandir Maidan in Ambedkar birthplace
 rahul ne kaha, 'desh main samvidhan ko lagu hue 65 saal ho gaye hai lekin ambedkar kaa jatvaad khatm karne kaa sapana aaj bhi adhuraa he
 Casteism still remains in our politics, our schools and our minds
 jati aapako skulon main acchhee shiksha paane or naukari hasil karne se roak sakati he
 ' congress upaadhyaksh ne jatvaad ko jad se ukhaad phenkane kaa aahvaan karte hue kaha, ambedkar bahut pehle kah chuke the ki satta kaa vikendrikaran jatvaad ko kamjor karata he
 ' rahul ne kaha, 'bharat ko vikaas kii raah par aage badhaane ke liye hamen rojgaar or buniyadi dhaanche kii zarurat he, lekin jab tak kuch logon ko unke adhikaar se dur rakhaa jayega, tab tak desh apni puri kshamta hasil nahin kar saktaa
 ' congress upaadhyaksh ne samvidhan nirmaataa ko unki janmasthali par yaad karte hue kaha ki ambedkar ke yogadan ko desh or jati kii simaaon main nahin baandha saktaa
 Ambedkar did a lot of work in the interest of Dalits, but he was not just a leader of Dalits
 tippaniyan He said, 'ambedkar brought light to the lives of the Dalits and the weaker sections of the society, he hit the thousands of years old wall of casteism
 vah atyaachaar ke khilaaf virodh ke vaishvik pratik the
 He was also a major contributor to empowering women and laborers and establishing the Reserve Bank of India
 ' Rahul said, 'ambedkar together with Mahatma Gandhi, Jawaharlal Nehru and Maulana Azad laid the foundation of independent India

 But do you know which are the five most frightening pictures of destruction in independent India? Look 
 
 -uttarakhand main 2013 main aasamaani sailaab, 10 hazaar se zyada maut-gujarat ke bhuj main 2001 main bukamp, 20 hazaar maut-maharashtra ke latur main 1993 main bukamp, 20 hazaar maut-dakshin bharat main 2004 main tsunami, 13 hazaar maut-jammu-kashmir ke laddakh main 2010 main aasamaani sailaab, aadha shahar tabah

 qudarat ke qahar ne kai-kai baar anginat zindagiyon ko hameshaa ke liye khamosh kar diya

 Five most terrifying pictures of natural havoc in Azad Hindustan
 
 
 wo tasviir jo jab-jab ankhon ke saamne se guzarati he, ankhen nam ho jaati hai
 Here are five of the most frightening stories of natural havoc in independent India
 
 
 uttarakhand ke nau zile, das hazaar maut kaa andeshaadesh main bhagwaan shiv ke sabase bade sthaan main se ek kedarnath
 When the glacier surfaced from the back of the same Kedarnath temple, the scene became frightening
 ek baar jaise hi laharon ne kedarnath mandir ko paar kiya, phir to inke tevar dekhne laayak the
 Whoever came in the way, got swept away
 afat aasmaan ne barasaai

 aisi belgaum ki ghar-naale, pahaad, sadak, raste, pul sabhi tabah ho gaye
 The gharande collapses like cards, the localities of the area turning into crematoriums
 manjilon tak pahunchane vaale raste jab khud hi mit jate hai, tab sirf ek hi manzar bachataa he, tabaahi kaa manjar, dard kaa manzar, bechaargi-bebarasi kaa manzar
 What a flood it was, which made everything watery
 kaisaa sailaab tha, jisane basti kii basti ujaad di

 sirf ek raat ke kahar ne uttarakhand ke nau jilon main tabaahi kii wo ibaarat likh di, jo ab hameshaa-hameshaa ke liye itihaas ke pannon main darj ho jayega

 puri kii puri kedaar ghati main sirf shiv hi bache the, baaqi kuch bhi nahin

 yahi manzar garbhagrih kaa bhi tha

 yah kudarat se khilwaad kaa nateeja tha yaa phir badal fatne kaa anjaam, vinaash ke prabhu shiv kaa krodh tha yaa phir achaanak ai aapadaa, iskaa hisaab-qitaab to hona abhi baaqi he
 But some calculations suggest that more than a thousand roads, over five hundred bridges and thousands of rough-paved paths have been erased out of the nine districts of Uttarakhand
 rahi bachi jindagiyon kii baat, to laashon kii ginati to phir bhi mumkin he, par unka kya, jinaki zindagi ab jinda rahakar bhi maut se badtar ho gai he

 7 on the Richter scale
 7 kii tivrata se subah 8 bajkar 46 minute par aae is bukamp main 20 hajaar se zyada logon kii jaane chali gayi
 1 lakh 67 thousand people were injured and about 6 lakh people were made homeless

 logon ke pair dagamagane lage

 aap mobile istemaal karte hue achaanak dekhte hai ki aapke phone kaa signal gaayab ho gaya
 Troubled, you were wondering what to do that only when the signal comes back and a phone comes with it
 phone karne vaala bataata he ki wo usee mobile company se bol rahaa he jiskaa SIM card aap istemaal kar rahe hai
 He asks you if there was a problem with your phone? Obviously, you answer yes
 phone karne vaala kahata he ki aisa isliye ho rahaa he kyonki network main kuch dikkat aa rahi he ise thik karne kii jarurat he
 You ask what needs to be done for this
 phone karne vaala aapako bataata he ki apane phone par "ek'' number dabaaie
 Or he tells you that a message will be sent to your phone right now, and you have to reply by pressing "1", which will reset the network and remove the problem
 aap fouran aisa karne ko taiyaar ho jate hai kyonki aap phone nahin chalane ko lekar pareshaan hai
 But shortly after sending the message on the phone, your phone's network disappears again
 agle din aapako pataa chalata he ki aapkaabank acountkhaali kiya ja chukaa he or usamen se saare paise nikal gaye hai
 Your phone was switched off, so neither a message came nor did you know at that time
 aaj lagbhag har vyakti mobile phone istemaal kar rahaa he isiilie yah kahani har kisi ko daraa sakati he
 But right, a message claiming to be similar is becoming increasingly viral nowadays and people are warning each other about this on all whatsapp groups
 massej main likhaa gaya he ki hyderabad police kii sibar cell ne logon ko chetavanee di he ki agar aisa koi phone aae to katai ''ek'' number dabaane kii yaa phir koi massej bhejne kii galati naa karen
 This can cause your phone to be hacked while sitting
 massej main kahi gai baat chaunkaane vaali lekin saath hi sabko hi daraane vaali he
 We first approached the cyber cell of Hyderabad Police to do a viral test of this news, which is being claimed that this message came from them
 hamane dekha ki hyderabad police ke fasebuk pej par bhi yahi massej thik isi tarah se diya gaya he
 When we asked CS Raghuveer of ACP of Cyber cell of Hyderabad Police, he clearly said that this message has been posted on Facebook on behalf of those people and from there people are sharing it
 raghuveer ne kaha ki pichley 10 dinon ke bheetar hi aisi 4 shikaayatein un logon ke paas ai hai jisamen phone par hi logon kaa SIM card hack liya gaya or phir usase dupliket sim card banaakar bank se paise nikaale gaye
 ACP Raghuveer said that those people are investigating such cases and till now investigation has revealed that such calls came from Delhi
 dhokhe se sim card swap karne, yani dupliket sim bana lene ke bare main to sab ne suna he lekin kya yah sambhav he ki sirf phone par massej bhej kar yaa kuch batan dabaane se aapke sim card kii jaankaree duusari jagah pahunch jaae or aapkaa dupliket sim card bana liya jaae?jab hamane is bare main sibar security ke visheshgyon se baat kii to pataa chalaa ki aisa karnaa aasaan to nahin he lekin asambhav bhi nahin he
 When we asked Cyber security expert Saket Modi about this, he said that he had never dealt with such a case, but it cannot be said that this is not possible
 lekin jab hamane iske bare main or tahakikat kii to pataa chalaa ki kai saal pehle duniya ke jane maane sibar security export germany ke carston nol ne is bare main apni ek research pesh karte hue kaha tha ki bina phone ke sampark main aae, dur se bhi sim card ko hack kiya ja saktaa he
 He did his research in 2013 and warned that many mobile companies are still using SIM cards based on old technology which can be hacked by sending only messages
 nol ke is research ki us vakt kaaphi charchaa hui thi or ise sibar security ke liye vikhyath blike hat conference main pesh bhi kiya gaya tha
 All banks continue to warn their customers about stealing SIM information
 ab sawaal yah uthta he ki sim card dupliket ban jane se bank acount se paise kaise nikal sakate hai
 Actually, criminals who hack SIM cards target the same people whose bank details and all other information are already with them
 aise apradhi kai charnon main apana kaam karte hai or apana shikaar usee hisaab se chunate hai
 # First of all, they collect all information related to someone's name, address, phone number and bank account through fake mail and message or through phishing
 # phir ye log us vyakti ke bare main fasebuk, twitor jaise soshal media se uske bare main sari jaankaree jaise - janmdin, parivaar ke logon kaa naam, aadhaar card number, pan number or tamaam duusari jaankariyaan jutate hai
 Based on these information, they try to guess the bank's password or reset the password based on all the information
 yahaan par ab otipi kii jarurat padati he jiske liye sim card kaam aata he
 # Then on the basis of fake identity card these people get another duplicate sim card in the name of the same person for which they inform the mobile operator that their phone or sim card has been lost
 # dupliket sim card haath main aa jane ke baad yah log bank acount main log in karte hai or dupliket sim ke dam par otipi bhi paa lete hai
 Meanwhile, due to the phone being switched off, the person who has a bank account is unable to know that the OTP duplicate of his bank account is coming on the SIM card and money is coming out of his bank
 # jab tak vyakti mobile company yaa bank tak pahunchataa he tab tak apradhi apana kaam karke chanpat ho jate hai
 People associated with cyber experts and bank security insist on taking care of some things to avoid such deception
 1
 Thoughtfully open the email of any unknown person, especially if there is any attachment in it, do not open it at all
 isse koi software aapke computer yaa phir aapke phone main downlod ho saktaa he
 After this, every information will continue to reach the hacker without your knowledge
 2
 Do not give details of your bank in response to any email even if the person seeking information claims to be an employee of the bank
 shaq hone par khud bank ko phone karke pataa karen yaa phir police ko us number kii jaankaree den
 Neither send any message nor press any phone button
 3
 To log in to your bank account, type the address of the bank account directly
 kabhi bhi kisi email main die gaye pate ke aadhaar par bank kii site par nahin jaaen
 This may be a fake site
 4
 Thoughtfully enter any information on social media because anyone can take advantage of this information incorrectly
 5
 Sometimes if the phone suddenly starts ringing on the phone and someone rings the bell continuously, then never stop getting fed up and be careful

 30 baje ok creek sthit gurudware main hui golibari kii ghatana ko gharelu aatankwaad jaisi ek ghatana maani ja rahi he
 The officer who was the first to respond was also injured in the incident
 edwards ne kaha ki ok creek ke jo police adhikari 911 kii kol ke jawaab main gaye the, ve ek peedit kii madad kar rahe the tabhi hamalavar ne unamem se ek adhikari par hamalaa bol diya or us par kai goliyaan barasaai
 In response, another police officer fired and killed the attacker
 jarnal centinel ne jaanch se sambandhit ek sutara ke hawaale se kaha he ki hamalavar shwet purush tha, jisaki umr 40 varsh ke aasapaas rahi hogi
 He was retired from the army
 sutara ne kaha ki ghatnasthal se ek aagneyastra or kai magazine baraamad hue hai
 4 pm 30 baje adhikariyon se jaankaree milane ke baad obama ne governor scot vaakar, ok creek ke meyar steve skefidi or gurudware ke nyaasi charanjit singh ko phone kiya or mritkon ke prati shok samvednaa tathaa ghayalon ke prati chintaa jaahir kii
 Describing the Sikhs as a part of the broader American family, Obama promised in a statement issued by the White House that his administration would fully assist in investigating Sunday's incident
 obama ne kaha he, "ek dharmik sthal par ghati is ghatana par shok manaate hue hamen yaad he ki sikhon ne hamaare desh ko kitna samrudh banaaya he, jo hamaare vyapak america parivaar ke hissaa hai
 " obama ne kaha, "meraa prashasan ghatana kii jaanch se jude adhikariyon ko sabhi aavashyak madad muhaiyaa karaayega
 " obama ne kaha, "visconsin main golibari kii trasadpurn ghatana ke bare main sunakar mishael or mujhe gaharaa dukh hua
 " obama ke republican pratidwandvi mit romany ne boston main ise 'hinsa kii nirmam karrwai' or ek traasadee qaraar diya, jise kisi bhi dharmik sthal par kabhi nahin ghatana chahie
 Romney said that he and his wife Anne are with heartbroken victims, their families and the entire Sikh community in Oak Creek
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne ghatana par gaharaa shok prakat karte hue aashaa vyakt kii he ki america prashasan hamale kii jaanch karegaa or yah sunishchit karaayega ki is tarah kii ghatana bhavishya main na ghate
 Speaking to reporters in the Parliament House, Manmohan said, "the brutal killing of people gathered in a religious gathering is a very sad incident
 " Manmohan said, "I hope the US administration will investigate the reasons behind this brutal attack on the devotees and ensure that such a horrific incident does not happen in future
" main aashaa karata hum ki sakasham adhikari ghatana kii jaanch karenge or prabhavit pariwaron ko raahat muhaiyaa karaayenge
 i express my heartfelt condolences to the families of those killed and injured in the incident
 " Foreign Minister SM Krishna has condemned the attack on Sunday at a gurdwara in the US
 unhone kaha ki america main sikh samudaay ne apane kaam ke prati khud ke drushtikon or patibaddhta ke jariye vahaan ke prashasan va logon kaa sammaan hasil kiya he
 Krishna said, "I condemn this incident
 " krishna ne kaha ki ghatana ke baad unhone bhartiya rajdoot nirupama raav se baat kii he
 Minister of State for External Affairs Praneet Kaur said that gurdwaras and other religious places in the community in America should be taken care of
 cor ne kaha, "yah ek bahut hi stabdhkaari or tragedeepurn ghatana ghati he, jo nindaneey he
 We are in equal contact with the US government and our Ambassador Nirupama Rao has sent a special officer from Washington to Wisconsin and Consul General in Chicago is also monitoring the case
 " The US embassy on Monday expressed deep grief over the incident that killed six Sikh devotees in an attack at a gurdwara in Wisconsin
 duutavas se jari bayaan main kaha gaya he, "america duutavas ke sadsy america or bharat ke sikh samudaay ke prati sahanubhuti evam shok samvednaa jaahir karne main raashtrapati (baraak) obama ke saath hai
 "comments bayaan main kaha gaya he, "hamaara hriday, hamaari aatma or prarthana peediton va unke parijanon ke saath he
 An investigation into the incident has begun
 is tarah kii koi bhi ghatana trasadpurn he, khaastaur se jab vah kisi dharmasthal par ghate
 America takes the responsibility of respect and protection of people of all religions very seriously
 " The statement said, "religious freedom and religious tolerance are fundamental pillars of American society
 america main sikh samudaay is siddhant main yogadan karata he or america ke saamaajik taane-bane ko arthpurna majbootee pradaan karata he
 " milwakee ke jarnal centinel main jari rapat ke anusaar, epabiai adhikariyon ne ravivaar raat is baat kii pushti kii thi ki ve ghatana ke sambandh main visconsin ke kudahi sthit ek ghar kii bhi jaanch kar rahe hai
 US Attorney James Santel was quoted as saying that it was unclear whether it was domestic terrorism
 unhone kaha, "meraa dhyaan is baat par nahin he ki yah kis shrenee kaa aparaadh he, balki dhyaan is ghatana par or logon kii maut par he
 " shahar ke police pramukh jon edwards ne kaha ki ravivaar subah lagbhag 10
 The shooting incident at the gurdwara at Oak Creek at 30 am is considered as an incident like domestic terrorism
 is ghatana main sarvapratham pratikriya dene vaala adhikari bhi ghayal ho gaya
 Edwards said police officers from Oak Creek who went in response to a 911 call were helping a victim when the attacker attacked one of the officers and fired several shots at him
 jawaab main ek duusare police adhikari ne golibari kar hamalavar ko maar daalaa
 The Journal Sentinel quoted a source as saying that the attacker was a white male, who must have been around 40 years of age
 vah sena se sevamukt ho gaya tha
 The source said that a firearms and several magazines have been recovered from the scene
 aparaahn 4
 At 30 pm, Obama received a call from Governor Scott Walker, Oak Creek Mayor Steve Scheffidi and Charanjit Singh, a trustee of the gurdwara, and expressed condolences to the dead and concern for the injured
 sikhon ko vyapak america parivaar kaa ek hissaa bataate hue obama ne white house kii ore se jari ek bayaan main vaada kiya ki ravivaar kii ghatana kii jaanch main unka prashasan puri madad karegaa
 Obama has said, "we mourn the incident at a religious site, remembering how prosperous the Sikhs have been to our country, who are part of our wider American family
" " Obama said, "my administration will provide all necessary help to the officers involved in the investigation of the incident
" " Obama said, "michelle and i were deeply saddened to hear of the tragic incident of the shooting in Wisconsin
 " Obama's Republican rival Mitt Romney called it a 'ruthless action of violence' and a tragedy in Boston, which should never happen at any religious site
 romany ne kaha ki vah or unki patni ain hriday se peediton, unke pariwaron or puure ok creek ke sikh samudaay ke saath hai
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh expressed deep condolences over the incident and hoped that the US administration would investigate the attack and ensure that such incidents do not happen in future
 sansad bhawan main samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main manmohan ne kaha, "dharmik sabha main jamaa hue logon kii nirmam hatya bahut hi dukhad ghatana he
 " manmohan ne kaha, "mujhe aashaa he ki america prashasan shraddhaluon par hue is krur hamale ke peeche ke kaarnon kii jaanch karegaa or yah sunishchit karaayega ki is tarah kii khaufnak ghatana bhavishya main na ho
 i hope that the competent authorities will investigate the incident and provide relief to the affected families
 ghatana main maare gaye or ghayal hue logon ke parijanon ke prati main apni hardik samvednaa vyakt karata hum
 " videsh mantri esaem krishna ne america main ek gurudware main ravivaar ko hue hamale kii ninda kii he
 He said that the Sikh community in America has gained the respect of the administration and the people through its attitude and commitment to its work
 krishna ne kaha, "main is ghatana kii ninda karata hum
 "krishna said that he has spoken to Indian Ambassador Nirupama Rao after the incident
 videsh rajya mantri pranit cor ne kaha ki america main sthit gurudwaron or samudaay ke anya dharmik sthalon kaa khyaal rakhaa janaa chahie
 Kaur said, "it has been a very shocking and tragic incident, which is condemnable
" ham america sarkaar se baraabar sampark main hai or hamaari rajdoot nirupama raav ne washington se ek vishesh adhikari ko visconsin bheja he tathaa chicago main mahavanijyadoot bhi maamle par najar rakhe hue hai
 " america duutavas ne visconsin ke gurudware main hue hamale main chah sikh shraddhaluon ke maare jane kii ghatana par somvaar ko gaharaa dukh vyakt kiya
 The statement issued from the embassy said, "the members of the US embassy are with President (barack) Obama in expressing sympathy and condolences to the Sikh community of America and India
" "tippaniyan The statement said, "our heart, our soul and prayers are with the victims and their families
 ghatana kii jaanch shuru ho gai he
 Any such incident is tragic, especially when it happens at a shrine
 america sabhi dharm ke logon ke sammaan or hifaazat kii jimmedaari bahut gambheertha se letaa he
 " bayaan main kaha gaya he, "dharmik aazaadee or dharmik sahishnutaa america samaaj ke buniyadi stambh hai

 " aparaahn 4
 At 30 pm, Obama received a call from Governor Scott Walker, Oak Creek Mayor Steve Scheffidi and Charanjit Singh, a trustee of the gurdwara, and expressed condolences to the dead and concern for the injured
 sikhon ko vyapak america parivaar kaa ek hissaa bataate hue obama ne white house kii ore se jari ek bayaan main vaada kiya ki ravivaar kii ghatana kii jaanch main unka prashasan puri madad karegaa
 Obama has said, "we mourn the incident at a religious site, remembering how prosperous the Sikhs have been to our country, who are part of our wider American family
" " Obama said, "my administration will provide all necessary help to the officers involved in the investigation of the incident
" " Obama said, "michelle and i were deeply saddened to hear of the tragic incident of the shooting in Wisconsin
 " Obama's Republican rival Mitt Romney called it a 'ruthless action of violence' and a tragedy in Boston, which should never happen at any religious site
 romany ne kaha ki vah or unki patni ain hriday se peediton, unke pariwaron or puure ok creek ke sikh samudaay ke saath hai
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh expressed deep condolences over the incident and hoped that the US administration would investigate the attack and ensure that such incidents do not happen in future
 sansad bhawan main samvaadadaataaon se baatcheet main manmohan ne kaha, "dharmik sabha main jamaa hue logon kii nirmam hatya bahut hi dukhad ghatana he
 " manmohan ne kaha, "mujhe aashaa he ki america prashasan shraddhaluon par hue is krur hamale ke peeche ke kaarnon kii jaanch karegaa or yah sunishchit karaayega ki is tarah kii khaufnak ghatana bhavishya main na ho
 i hope that the competent authorities will investigate the incident and provide relief to the affected families

 " videsh mantri esaem krishna ne america main ek gurudware main ravivaar ko hue hamale kii ninda kii he
 He said that the Sikh community in America has gained the respect of the administration and the people through its attitude and commitment to its work

 "krishna said that he has spoken to Indian Ambassador Nirupama Rao after the incident

 aise main isamen vitamin bi kii prachur maatra hoti he
 Vitamin b works to nourish hair and scalp
 isamen maujuud maltose or glucose baalo ko majbootee dete hai
 But for all these benefits, it is very important to know how to wash hair with beer: 1
 acchhee quality kii bear khariden:aakhirkaar ye aapke baalo kaa sawaal he
 In such a situation, do not compromise the quality of the beer for a few cents
 bear kii bottle par uske banane or expire hone kii date jarur dekh len
 2
 saamaanya taapmaana par rakhen:bear se bal dhone ke kuch ghante pehle hi aap bear kii bottle ko refricrator se baahar nikaalkar rakh den
 When the bottle becomes normal, wash hair with it
 3
 Shampoo in hair: After this wash your hair with daily used shampoo
 par bhuulakar bhi condishnar na lagaaein
 Baby shampoo is best used for shampooing hair
 4
 Pour the beer on the head: After this, pour the beer on your head depending on the length of your hair
 use halke haathon se scalp par malein
 But too much rubbing can cause hair loss
 5
 Now wash hair: Wash hair thoroughly with water but do not rub at all
 aisa karne se baalo ko nuksaan ho saktaa he
 6
 karen condishnar kaa istemaal:haalanki bear ek natural condishnar he lekin agar aapako lagata he ki bear kaa istemaal karne ke baad bhi aapako puri softness nahin mil pai he to aap thodaa sa condishnar istemaal kar sakate hai
